)@@G@@.     @G@@@@. DYNAMIC SEGMENT MCORE$ ROUTINE - ADAPTED FROM 'DLOAD$' RLIIM
)@@G@@B$ ELEMENT  @[@@@@.     @F@@@@DSEG*     LSSL      A1,2              CONVIN
)@@G@@ERT SEGID TO SLT INDEX  @E@@@@          A,U       A1,SLT$           GET IO
)@@G@@ADDR OF SLT ENTRY @F@@@@          L,S2      A0,,A1            TEST IF SEIP
)@@G@@G DEFINED AS DSEG @ @@@@          TE,U      A0,011    @ @@@@          TNIQ
)@@G@@E,U     A0,010    @E@@@@          J         $+2               IS A DSEG IR
)@@G@@- CONTINUE  @D@@@@          ER        EABT$             MUST BE A DSEG  IS
)@@G@@@E@@@@          L,H1      A0,1,A1           LOAD IBANK ADDR NEEDED@G@@@@IT
)@@G@@          L,S2      A2,SLT$           DETERMINE IF SLT FORMAT COMPLEX   IU
)@@G@@@ @@@@          TNE,U     A2,022    @E@@@@          J         DLOAD0    IV
)@@G@@        IF COMPLEX, DLOAD0    @E@@@@          JZ        A0,$+3          IW
)@@G@@  CHECK FOR VOID SEGMENT@G@@@@          A         A0,(1*/34)        SET IX
)@@G@@PROGRAM-WIDE BIT FOR MCORE    @D@@@@          ER        MCORE$          IY
)@@G@@  EXPAND IBANK    @E@@@@          L,H1      A0,2,A1           LOAD DBANKIZ
)@@G@@ ADDR NEEDED@E@@@@          JZ        A0,DLOAD2         CHECK FOR VOID SJA
)@@G@@EG    @D@@@@          A         A0,(1*/34)        SET PGM-WIDE BIT@D@@@@JB
)@@G@@          ER        MCORE$            EXPAND DBANK    @C@@@@          J JC
)@@G@@        DLOAD2            CONTINUE  @F@@@@DLOAD0    L         A2,A1     JD

)@@G@@        CHECK FOR VOID SEG    @E@@@@          LXI,T1    A0,2,A2         JF
)@@G@@  LOAD BDI FOR THIS BANK@D@@@@          A         A0,(1*/34)        SET JG
)@@G@@PGM-WIDE BIT@D@@@@          ER        MCORE$            EXPAND BANK     JH
)@@G@@@F@@@@          L,H2      A2,2,A2           LOAD LINK TO NEXT EXTENSION JI
)@@G@@@F@@@@          JZ        A2,DLOAD2         JUMP IF ALL EXTENSIONS DONE JJ

)@@G@@          L,H1      A0,1,A2           LOAD BANK ADDR NEEDED @F@@@@      JL
)@@G@@    J         DLOAD1            CONTINUE EXPANSION LOOP     @F@@@@DLOAD2JM
)@@G@@    L,U       A2,024            MARK SEG AS OVERLAY SEG     @ @@@@      JN
)@@G@@    S,S2      A2,,A1    @C@@@@          J         0,X11             RETUJO
)@@G@@RN    @#@@@@          END     ___B@@@@@@@@0586AA*[S@@@*SDFF*@^@@@@. @MFDJP

)@@G@@IN2000* .  PHASE 2 OF @MFD INITIALIZATION @[@@@@.     @F@@@@. GET USER'SNW
)@@G@@ PCT.  CHECK FOR ILLEGAL USE OF PRIVILEGED OPTIONS    @[@@@@.     @D@@@@NX

)@@G@@        IS T-OPTION REVERSED? @H@@@@          SA        A0,REVT         OV

)@@G@@    J         IN2130            YES @D@@@@          J         IN2140    PO
)@@G@@        NO, SO GO ON    @[@@@@.     @F@@@@. D-OPTION ROUTINE - DO TREAD PP
)@@G@@TO PICK UP DATE TO CHECK AGAINST    @[@@@@.     @D@@@@IN2100    LA,U    PQ
)@@G@@  A0,TPKT           GET TREAD PACKET@D@@@@          ER        TREAD$    PR
)@@G@@        ASK FOR DATE    @E@@@@          SA        A0,A1             SAVEPS
)@@G@@ INPUT WORD COUNT @C@@@@          P$RINT    PPKT              ECHO REPLYPT
)@@G@@@D@@@@          LA,U      A0,,A1            INPUT WORD COUNT@C@@@@      PU

)@@G@@TION ROUTINE - REQUEST PARAMETER FOR TYPE OF DISABLE TO CHECK     @[@@@@QN

)@@G@@UCTION TABLE - CREATED BY INIT1, AND EXECUTED   @^@@@@. BY 'CHECK' ROUTIZX
)@@G@@NE.   @[@@@@.     @E@@@@.     FOR SINGLE-WORD SPECS            FOR DOUBLZY

)@@G@@LENGTH@E@@@@SSTAB*    RES       SSIZE*NSSP        RESERVE TABLE SPACE   AE

)@@G@@SSP>5)*(2*5)@^@@@@ADDKEYS*  RES       KEYL@ @@@@          ON        BRKOFB
)@@G@@K     @[@@@@.     @G@@@@. BRKTBL WILL CONTAIN THE NECESSARY INSTRUCTIONSFC
)@@G@@ AND DATA TO PROVIDE THE@H@@@@. SUBTOTAL ('BREAK') FEATURE.  EACH ENTRY FD

)@@G@@             DOUBLE WORD              SINGLE BIT@F@@@@.     ----------- FG

)@@G@@>,X8         DL  A0,<D>,X8            LA,<J> A0,<D>,X8@H@@@@.  1  TE    FI

)@@G@@LUE   @G@@@@.  3  <UNUSED>                 +   FORMER VALUE         +   FL

)@@G@@AL WORD DESIGNATOR, IF ANY, AND <D> IS THE OFFSET     @G@@@@. INTO THE SFP

)@@G@@@C@@@@. EDIT A LETTER INDICATING FILE @ASG STATE:     @C@@@@. BLANK - FITU
)@@G@@LE NOT CURRENTLY ASSIGNED TO ANYONE @C@@@@.     A - FILE ASSIGNED TO AT TV
)@@G@@LEAST ONE RUN     @C@@@@.     X - FILE EXCLUSIVELY ASSIGNED TO SOME RUN TW
)@@G@@@E@@@@.     C - (SINGLE-FILE MODE ONLY) FILE @ASG,C BY THIS RUN   @E@@@@TX
)@@G@@.     U - (SINGLE-FILE MODE ONLY) FILE @ASG,U BY THIS RUN   @G@@@@.     TY
)@@G@@T - (SINGLE-FILE MODE ONLY) TEMPORARY FILE ASSIGNED TO THIS RUN   @[@@@@TZ
)@@G@@.     @D@@@@          LA        A0,CURASGCNT      GET ASG COUNT   @G@@@@UA
)@@G@@          TZ        SFASG             ASSIGNED FOR SINGLE-FILE DREAD$ ? UB

)@@G@@  YES - 1600 DENSITY?   @C@@@@          J         PR063             NO -UY
)@@G@@ SKIP @[@@@@.     @F@@@@. BIT 2**35 OF MI0+21 IS USED TO INDICATE 800-FPUZ
)@@G@@I MODE FOR DUAL-  @E@@@@. DENSITY 9-TRACK MSA TAPE DRIVES.  IT IS SET FOVA
)@@G@@R 800, CLEAR@E@@@@. FOR 1600.  THIS IS THE ONLY WAY TO CHECK FOR 'V' OPTVB
)@@G@@ION.  @E@@@@. HOWEVER, THIS BIT IS CLEAR FOR 7-TRACK MSA DRIVES, SO WE  VC
)@@G@@@F@@@@. MUST CHECK FOR 9-TRACK BEFORE ADDING THE 'V'.  I DON'T LIKE     VD
)@@G@@@D@@@@. THIS, SINCE IT RELIES ON THE 'OLD EQUIPMENT CODE'.  @[@@@@.     VE
)@@G@@@E@@@@          LA        A3,MI0OLDEQP      GET OLD EQUIPMENT CODE@E@@@@VF

)@@G@@QF000*  .   @[@@@@.     @D@@@@. SINGLE-FILE MODE WAS SPECIFIED, SO WE'LLTA
)@@G@@ GET THE    @E@@@@. INFORMATION ABOUT A PARTICULAR FILE WITHOUT DOING A TB
)@@G@@DGET$.@[@@@@.     @E@@@@. 1. FIRST, ATTACH AN INTERNAL NAME TO THE SPECITC
)@@G@@FIED FILE.  @F@@@@. 2. NOW TRY AN ER FITEM$ ON THAT FILE.  IF IT DOES NOTD
)@@G@@T WORK,     @G@@@@.    ASSIGN THE FILE, AND GO ON TO STEP 4.  IF THE FITTE
)@@G@@EM$ DOES WORK,    @B@@@@.    THE FILE IS ASSIGNED BY THE USER.    @F@@@@TF
)@@G@@. 3. USING INFO FROM FITEM$, CHECK FOR TAPE FILE, TEMPORARY FILE, @G@@@@TG
)@@G@@.    ARBITRARY DEVICE FILE (NOT TAPE OR MS), ETC., AND SET APPROPRIATE  TH
)@@G@@@F@@@@.    FLAGS.  IF FILE IS NOT TEMPORARY OR ARBITRARY DEVICE, GO ON  TI
)@@G@@@E@@@@.    TO STEP 4.  IF FILE IS TEMPORARY OR ARB DEVICE, CREATE @G@@@@TJ
)@@G@@.    FAKE LEAD ITEM AND MAIN ITEM BASED ON INFORMATION FROM FTIEM$.     TK
)@@G@@@ @@@@.    THEN GO ON TO STEP 5.    @F@@@@. 4. FILE IS CATALOGUED MASS STL
)@@G@@TORAGE OR TAPE FILE, AND MAY OR MAY @F@@@@.    NOT BE ASSIGNED BY THE USTM
)@@G@@ER.  AN ER MSCON$ IS NOW DONE, USING@G@@@@.    THE DREAD$ FUNCTION, TO OTN
)@@G@@BTAIN THE DIRECTORY INFORMATION FOR THIS  @F@@@@.    FILE.  FIRST THE LETO
)@@G@@AD ITEM IS READ, AND THEN THE MAIN ITEM.  @G@@@@.    CHECKS ARE MADE TO TP
)@@G@@DETERMINE WHETHER THE FILE IS REMOVABLE DISC,   @D@@@@.    TAPE, OR G-OPTQ
)@@G@@TION, AND APPROPRIATE FLAGS ARE SET.@G@@@@. 5. IF THE FILE IS NOT ASSIGNTR
)@@G@@ED BY THE USER, OR IF IT IS A TAPE FILE,  @H@@@@.    THIS STEP IS SKIPPETS
)@@G@@D.  IF NOT, WE LOAD THE RUN'S PCT BANK, VIA AN LDJ    @H@@@@.    (OR ER TT
)@@G@@PCT$), AND FIND THE FILE DESCRIPTION ENTRY FOR THIS FILE.  THIS   @F@@@@TU
)@@G@@.    IS THE ONLY WAY TO FIND THE GRANULE COUNTS AND PACKIDS FOR   @G@@@@TV
)@@G@@.    TEMPORARY FIXED AND REMOVABLE MASS STORAGE FILES, AND SOMETIMES    TW
)@@G@@@F@@@@.    PROVIDES MORE UP-TO-DATE GRANULE COUNTS FOR CATALOGUED FILES,TX
)@@G@@@G@@@@.    AS WELL.  AFTER GATHERING AS MUCH INFORMATION AS IS USEFUL FOTY
)@@G@@R THE @D@@@@.    SPECIFIC CASE, WE LDJ BACK TO THE NORMAL DBANK.  @G@@@@TZ
)@@G@@.    FOR TEMPORARY REMOVABLE DISC FILES, ADDITIONAL CODE IS NEEDED TO   UA
)@@G@@@G@@@@.    OBTAIN A COPY OF THE FASTRAND-FORMAT MASS STORAGE AVAILABILTYUB
)@@G@@ TABLE@F@@@@.    (FATBL), BECAUSE THE PCT ONLY HAS SUBSYSTEM AND UNIT NUUC
)@@G@@MBERS @F@@@@.    FOR THE DISC DRIVES INVOLVED, NOT THE PACKIDS.  FATBL MUD
)@@G@@UST BE@E@@@@.    SEARCHED AND CHECKED AGAINST THE PCT 'PACKID' TABLE.   UE
)@@G@@@F@@@@. 6. IF THE FILE IS TEMPORARY OR ARBITRARY DEVICE, THE @USE NAME  UF
)@@G@@@#@@@@.    IS NOW FREED.@G@@@@.    IF NOT, WE DETERMINE WHETHER OR NOT TUG
)@@G@@O FREE THE @USE RELATIONSHIP  @F@@@@.    NOW.  IF A SECOND PRINT LINE WIUH
)@@G@@LL BE NECESSARY FOR THE FILE, @F@@@@.    THEN WE WON'T FREE IT NOW:  ROUUI
)@@G@@TINE 'PRINT2' WILL FREE IT.   @[@@@@.     @F@@@@          L$OAD     CHEKUJ

)@@G@@**(LDJOK=0) @[@@@@.     @F@@@@. THIS SUBROUTINE IS FOR USE WHEN LDJ OF PNI
)@@G@@CT BANK IS NOT DESIRED  @F@@@@. (LDJOK EQU 0).  IT CONVERTS THE RELATVIENJ

)@@G@@         :  @B@@@@.     :<--  THIS PORTION IS SORTED  -->:  @[@@@@.     PQ
)@@G@@@G@@@@. TWO EXTRA WORDS ARE SORTED ALONG WITH LI0/MI0/MI1, TO SAVE FLAGSPR
)@@G@@, ETC.@[@@@@.     @H@@@@.     ------------------------------------------PS
)@@G@@-------------------------     @H@@@@.     :          :   BAK    :  RDISCPT
)@@G@@   :       TOTAL SIZE               :     @H@@@@.     ------------------PU
)@@G@@-------------------------------------------------     @H@@@@.     :     PV
)@@G@@                        FLAGS                               :     @H@@@@PW
)@@G@@.     ------------------------------------------------------------------PX
)@@G@@-     @[@@@@.     @C@@@@. 'BAK' IS BACKED-UP FLAG IN A13, AND 'RDISC'   PY
)@@G@@@F@@@@. IS REMOVABLE-DISC FLAG IN A14.  TOTAL SIZE IS NUMBER ACCUMULATEDPZ
)@@G@@@ @@@@. IN A15 BY 'CHECK' ROUTINE.  @[@@@@.     @^@@@@          AXR$    QA
)@@G@@  .   @G@@@@          CONFIG    .                 DEFINE CONFIGURATION PQB
)@@G@@ARAMETERS   @D@@@@          EQUFS     .                 DEFINE TAGS     QC
)@@G@@@ @@@@          ON        SORTOK    @E@@@@NREC      +         NFILES/2  QD
)@@G@@        NUMBER OF RECORDS     @E@@@@NCHAR     +         RECCHAR         QE
)@@G@@  CHARACTERS PER RECORD @[@@@@.     @B@@@@$(1). CALL SORTF TO ASSIGN SORQF
)@@G@@T FILES     @[@@@@.     @E@@@@OPNSRT*   SR        R15,SORTED        MARKQG
)@@G@@ SORT-SEG-LOADED  @E@@@@          LA,U      A0,NFILES         GET NUMBERQH
)@@G@@ OF FILES   @G@@@@          TZ        ZPT               PRIVILEGED AND DQI
)@@G@@OING EVERYTHING?  @F@@@@          SA        A0,NREC           YES, BETTEQJ
)@@G@@R INCREASE NREC   @D@@@@          DO        SRTDBG , P$RINT (0101,('SORTQK
)@@G@@F ')) @E@@@@          LMJ       X11,SORTF         ASSIGN SORT FILES     QL
)@@G@@@E@@@@          +         NREC              NUMBER OF RECORDS     @F@@@@QM
)@@G@@          +         NCHAR             NUMBER OF CHAR PER RECORD   @B@@@@QN
)@@G@@          +         0                 WB  @F@@@@NOSORTF*  R$OPN     SORTQO
)@@G@@BL            OPEN SORT, RETURN TO FPOC   @F@@@@. DON'T NEED PARAMETER CQP
)@@G@@ARD PROCESSING, SO REPLACE KPARCD WITH:   @[@@@@.     @ @@@@ROPN$*    LMQQ
)@@G@@J       X1,RSTRG$ @#@@@@          'ROPN$ '@ @@@@          J         RBPNQR
)@@G@@$     @]@@@@RTMIN$*   . @]@@@@RTMAX$*   . @]@@@@RTPT$*    . @]@@@@RTST$*QS
)@@G@@    . @]@@@@RTMT$*    . @]@@@@RLBLK$*   . @[@@@@.     @^@@@@. RELEASE REQT
)@@G@@CORD TO SORT@[@@@@.     @]@@@@GOTREC*   . @G@@@@          SA        BACKQU
)@@G@@EDUP,SAVEBAK  SAVE RDISC AND BACKED-UP FLAGS    @A@@@@          SA      QV
)@@G@@  RDISC,SAVERDISC @D@@@@          DO        SRTDBG , P$RINT (0101,('RRELQW
)@@G@@$ ')) @E@@@@          L,U       A0,RECSTART       PASS THIS FILE TO SORTQX
)@@G@@@^@@@@          R$REL     .   @G@@@@          J         CHK000          QY
)@@G@@  GET NEXT FILE (SEG IS LOADED)     @[@@@@.     @B@@@@. DIRSEC EOF HAS OQZ
)@@G@@CCURRED; DO THE SORT    @[@@@@.     @]@@@@DOSORT*   . @D@@@@          DORA
)@@G@@        SRTDBG , P$RINT (0101,('RSORT$')) @F@@@@          R$SORT    .   RB
)@@G@@              DO THE SORT, RETURN TO LPOC @]@@@@LPOC*     . @D@@@@      RC
)@@G@@    DO        SRTDBG , P$RINT (0101,('LPOC  ')) @[@@@@.     @F@@@@. GET RD
)@@G@@NEXT RECORD FROM SORT, AND JUMP TO PRINT ROUTINE WITH IT    @[@@@@.     RE
)@@G@@@]@@@@SRTNXT*   . @D@@@@          DO        SRTDBG , P$RINT (0101,('RRETRF
)@@G@@$ ')) @H@@@@          R$RET     SRTEOF          . GET NEXT RECORD - IF ERG
)@@G@@OF, GO TO SRTEOF  @F@@@@          LX,U      X8,,A0            POINT TO LRH
)@@G@@I0/MI0/MI1 ETC.   @F@@@@          LA        BACKEDUP,SAVEBAK  RETRIEVE RRI
)@@G@@DISC, BAK FLAGS   @A@@@@          LA        RDISC,SAVERDISC @D@@@@      RJ
)@@G@@    LA        FILESIZE,SAVESIZE RETRIEVE SIZE   @H@@@@          J       RK
)@@G@@  PR000             JUMP TO PRINT ROUTINE (SEG IS LOADED)   @[@@@@.     RL
)@@G@@@A@@@@. EOF STATUS RECEIVED FROM SORT     @[@@@@.     @E@@@@SRTEOF    TNRM
)@@G@@Z       SFMODE2           SINGLE-FILE MODE?     @E@@@@          J       RN
)@@G@@  MFD600            NO, RETURN TO MAIN SEG@F@@@@          J         QF90RO
)@@G@@0             YES, RETURN FOR ANOTHER FILE@ @@@@          OFF       SORTRP
)@@G@@OK    @#@@@@          END     ___ERS PER RECORD @[@@@@.     @B@@@@$(1). RQ
)@@G@@CALL SORTF TO ASSIGN SOR*[S@@@*SDFF*@^@@@@          AXR$      .   @[@@@@RR
)@@G@@.     @F@@@@.         SORTF - FORTRAN CALLABLE ROUTINE TO ASSIGN SORT FIRS
)@@G@@LES   @[@@@@.     @B@@@@.         ORIGINALLY BY WALT GILBERT (UOM)@D@@@@RT
)@@G@@.         UPDATED BY R. DUFF KURLAND (ISD) TO PROVIDE:@[@@@@.     @B@@@@RU
)@@G@@.           - EXEC LEVEL 33 COMPATABILITY @C@@@@.           - REMOVABLE RV
)@@G@@DISC USAGE FOR XB FILE  @[@@@@.     @H@@@@.         IF AN 'XB' FILE IS NRW
)@@G@@EEDED, IT WILL BE ASSIGNED ON TYPE <FIXTYPE>,   @G@@@@.         UNLESS TRX
)@@G@@HE MAXIMUM DRUM FILE SIZE (XBMAXF) IS EXCEEDED, OR THE@H@@@@.         RERY
)@@G@@QUIRED NUMBER OF POSITIONS EXCEEDS THE AMOUNT CURRENTLY AVAILABLE.@G@@@@RZ
)@@G@@.         IN THIS CASE, 'XB' WILL BE ASSIGNED ON A REMOVABLE DISC, USINGSA
)@@G@@@H@@@@.         EQUIPMENT TYPE <REMTYPE>, AND PACKID <REMPACK>.  IF NO RSB
)@@G@@EMOVABLE    @G@@@@.         DISC ASSIGNS ARE DESIRED, <REMTYPE> SHOULD BSC
)@@G@@E SET TO ZERO.    @[@@@@.     @H@@@@.         IF A REMOVABLE ASSIGN OF 'SD
)@@G@@XB' IS ATTEMPTED AND FAILS (DUE TO THE    @G@@@@.         DRIVE NOT BEINSE
)@@G@@G AVAILABLE, ETC.), SORTF WILL REVERT TO A FIXED@H@@@@.         ASSIGN, SF
)@@G@@BUT WITHOUT THE INITIAL RESERVE.  FURTHERMORE, IF THE FILE  @H@@@@.     SG
)@@G@@    IS LESS THAN <XBREVP> POSITIONS, TRACK GRANULARITY WILL BE USED.    SH
)@@G@@@G@@@@.         THIS IS ALL TO MINIMIZE THE SYSTEM IMPACT OF A SORT WHENSI
)@@G@@ MASS @B@@@@.         STORAGE AVAILABILITY IS LOW.    @[@@@@.     @F@@@@SJ
)@@G@@REMTYPE   EQU       0                 TYPE FOR REMOVABLE XB ASGS  @E@@@@SK
)@@G@@.                                     MUST BE 3 CHARS, RJSF @G@@@@FIXTYPSL
)@@G@@E   EQU       'F40'             TYPE TO USE FOR FIXED XB ASGS     @D@@@@SM
)@@G@@.                                     (3 CHARS, RJSF) @H@@@@REMPACK   EQSN
)@@G@@U       'TEMP00'          PACKID FOR REMOVABLE XB ASGS (LJSF)     @F@@@@SO
)@@G@@.                                     IGNORED IF REMTYPE = 0.     @H@@@@SP
)@@G@@XBMAXF    EQU       0                 MAX SIZE OF FIXED XB FILE (POSITIOSQ
)@@G@@NS)   @F@@@@.                                     IGNORED IF REMTYPE = 0SR
)@@G@@.     @F@@@@XBMAX     EQU       150               MAX XB SIZE, ANY ASG TSS
)@@G@@YPE   @F@@@@.                                     (ONLY TO PREVENT ABUSEST
)@@G@@)     @F@@@@MSIZE     EQU       300               MSALL$ FATBL BUFFER SISU
)@@G@@ZE    @[@@@@.     @C@@@@RTYPE     EQU       ('.,'*/24)+(REMTYPE*/6)+'/' SV
)@@G@@@C@@@@FTYPE     EQU       ('.,'*/24)+(FIXTYPE*/6)+'/' @[@@@@.     @A@@@@SW
)@@G@@.         ALL FILES ARE FREED FIRST @[@@@@.     @^@@@@FREXA     '@FREE XSX
)@@G@@A    '@^@@@@FREXB     '@FREE XB    '@^@@@@FRECOR    '@FREE R$CORE'@[@@@@SY
)@@G@@.     @ @@@@.         XA FILE ASSIGN IMAGE@[@@@@.     @A@@@@ASGXA     '@SZ
)@@G@@ASG,T    XA.,F///******'@ @@@@ASGXAL    EQU       $-ASGXA   @[@@@@.     TA
)@@G@@@A@@@@.         XB FILE ASSIGN IMAGES     @[@@@@.     @[@@@@.     @G@@@@TB
)@@G@@.         NORMAL (FIXED) XB ASSIGN, EXTENDED FOR REMOVABLE ASSIGN IF    TC
)@@G@@@A@@@@.         CONFIGURED AND NECESSARY. @[@@@@.     @B@@@@ASGXB     '@TD
)@@G@@ASG,T    XB.,FXX/***/POS/*** '@G@@@@ASGXBL    EQU       $-ASGXB         TE
)@@G@@  LENGTH OF NORMAL XB ASSIGN IMAGE  @ @@@@          ON        REMTYPE   TF
)@@G@@@H@@@@XBPACK    +         REMPACK           PACKID TAGGED ONTO END OF XBTG
)@@G@@ ASG IMAGE  @G@@@@DISC      +         0                 NONZERO IF REMOVTH
)@@G@@ABLE ASG NEEDED   @[@@@@.     @F@@@@.         REMOTE EXECUTE TABLE TO STTI
)@@G@@UFF COMMA AFTER MAX GRANS     @[@@@@.     @F@@@@COMMA     S,S2      A0,ATJ
)@@G@@SGXB+4        FOR MAX = INITIAL = 1 DIGIT @F@@@@          S,S4      A0,ATK
)@@G@@SGXB+4        FOR MAX = INITIAL = 2 DIGITS@F@@@@          S,S6      A0,ATL
)@@G@@SGXB+4        FOR MAX = INITIAL = 3 DIGITS@[@@@@.     @E@@@@.         XBTM
)@@G@@ ASSIGN IMAGE USED WHEN REMOVABLE ASSIGN FAILS. @[@@@@.     @B@@@@ASGXB2TN
)@@G@@    '@ASG,T    XB.,FXX//POS/ ******'@ @@@@ASGXB2L   EQU       $-ASGXB2  TO
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @G@@@@XBREVP    EQU       10                POINT AT WHICH TTP
)@@G@@O STOP SWITCHING  @E@@@@.                                     TO TRACK GTQ
)@@G@@RANULARITY  @ @@@@          OFF       REMTYPE   @[@@@@.     @ @@@@.     TR
)@@G@@    R$CORE ASSIGN IMAGE @[@@@@.     @A@@@@ASGCOR    '@ASG,T R$CORE.,F2//TS
)@@G@@/**  '@ @@@@ASGCORL   EQU       $-ASGCOR  @[@@@@.     @^@@@@.         MSTT
)@@G@@ALL$ PACKET @[@@@@.     @G@@@@MSPKT     +         1,MSALL$          LEVETU
)@@G@@L-33 FORMAT MSCON$/MSALL$ CALL@E@@@@          +         MSIZE,MSBUF     TV
)@@G@@  BUFFER LENGTH, ADDRESS@D@@@@          +         0                 FILLTW
)@@G@@ED BY MSCON$@D@@@@          +         0                 FILLED BY MSCON$TX
)@@G@@@D@@@@          +         0                 FILLED BY MSCON$@[@@@@.     TY
)@@G@@@F@@@@MSBEG     EQUF      MSPKT+3,,H1       STARTING MS DEVICE INDEX    TZ
)@@G@@@E@@@@MSEND     EQUF      MSPKT+3,,H2       LAST MS DEVICE INDEX  @F@@@@UA
)@@G@@DSCBEG    EQUF      MSPKT+4,,H1       STARTING DISC DEVICE INDEX  @E@@@@UB
)@@G@@DSCEND    EQUF      MSPKT+4,,H2       LAST DISC DEVICE INDEX@[@@@@.     UC
)@@G@@@ @@@@.         MSALL$ FATBL BUFFER @[@@@@.     @F@@@@MSBUF     RES     UD
)@@G@@  MSIZE             RESERVE SPACE FOR FATBL     @[@@@@.     @E@@@@SAV   UE
)@@G@@    RES       1                 SAVE AREA FOR A10     @[@@@@.     @B@@@@UF
)@@G@@E(1)      'RECORD SIZE NEGATIVE OR ZERO'. @C@@@@E(2)      'NUMBER OF RECUG
)@@G@@ORDS NEGATIVE OR ZERO'. @D@@@@E(3)      'XXXXXX POSITIONS IS TOO LARGE FUH
)@@G@@OR SORTF'.  @E@@@@E(4)      'SORT FILE ASSIGN REJECTED:    XXXXXXXXXXXX'UI
)@@G@@.     @G@@@@E(5)      ' ONLY XXXXXX TRACKS OF STORAGE  REMAIN,   SORT NEUJ
)@@G@@EDS  XXXXXX'@E@@@@E(6)      ' ONLY XXXXXX POSITIONS REMAIN, SORT NEEDS XUK
)@@G@@XXXXX'@D@@@@E(7)      'SORTF ERROR - MSALL$ BUFFER IS TOO SMALL.' @B@@@@UL
)@@G@@E(8)      'SORTF MSCON$ ERROR CODE XX'    @]@@@@E(9)      . @^@@@@I     UM
)@@G@@    DO        8 ,;@F@@@@EE(I)     + 0200+E(I+1)-E(I),E(I).    GENERATE PUN
)@@G@@RINT CONTROL WORDS@F@@@@XA        +         0                 XA (SMALL)UO
)@@G@@ FILE SIZE, TRK   @F@@@@XB        +         0                 XB (LARGE)UP
)@@G@@ FILE SIZE, POS   @G@@@@CORE      +         0                 CORE SIZE,UQ
)@@G@@ THOUSANDS OF WORDS     @[@@@@.     @A@@@@.         MERGE POWER LLOKUP TUR
)@@G@@ABLE  @[@@@@.     @B@@@@MGPS      +         2                 4   @B@@@@US
)@@G@@          +         5                 5   @B@@@@          +         9   UT
)@@G@@              6   @B@@@@          +         17                7   @B@@@@UU
)@@G@@          +         26                8   @B@@@@          +         37  UV
)@@G@@              9   @B@@@@          +         53                10  @B@@@@UW
)@@G@@          +         72                11  @B@@@@          +         94  UX
)@@G@@              12  @B@@@@          +         121               13  @B@@@@UY
)@@G@@          +         153               14  @B@@@@          +         190 UZ
)@@G@@              15  @B@@@@          +         232               16  @B@@@@VA
)@@G@@          +         280               17  @B@@@@          +         335 VB
)@@G@@              18  @B@@@@          +         395               19  @B@@@@VC
)@@G@@          +         460               20  @B@@@@          +         530 VD
)@@G@@              21  @F@@@@NMGPS     EQU       $-MGPS.           NUMBER OF VE
)@@G@@ENTRIES IN TABLE  @[@@@@.     @F@@@@RETURN    +         0               VF
)@@G@@  RETURN ADDRESS STORE HERE   @[@@@@/$(1).@]@@@@SORTF*    . @ @@@@      VG
)@@G@@    S         A10,SAV   @G@@@@          L,U       A1,'WJG'          LOADVH
)@@G@@ @SORTF CALL IDENTITY FLAG    @H@@@@          SZ        A4              VI
)@@G@@  SET FLAG. 0=SUBROUTINE CALL, _0=@SORTF  @G@@@@          TNE,H2    A1,2VJ
)@@G@@,X11          IS THIS SORTF-DRIVER CALLING?     @H@@@@          L       VK
)@@G@@  A4,2,X11          YES, LOAD ENTIRE WORD TO GET SIGN FLAG  @H@@@@      VL
)@@G@@    JN        A4,NOCSF          DON'T ISSUE CSF$'S IF 'X' OPTION ON     VM
)@@G@@@H@@@@          L         A0,(2,FREXA)      FREE ALL OF THE FILES: XA, XVN
)@@G@@B, R$CORE   @^@@@@          ER        CSF$@A@@@@          L         A0,(VO
)@@G@@2,FREXB)    @^@@@@          ER        CSF$@A@@@@          L         A0,(VP
)@@G@@2,FRECOR)   @^@@@@          ER        CSF$@E@@@@NOCSF     L,U       A0,3VQ
)@@G@@,X11          GET RETURN ADDRESS    @C@@@@          S,H2      A0,RETURN VR
)@@G@@        SAVE IT.  @F@@@@          L         A1,*1,X11         LOAD RECORVS
)@@G@@D SIZE IN CHARS   @E@@@@          JN        A1,ERR2           ERROR IF NVT
)@@G@@EGATIVE     @ @@@@          A,U       A1,11 .   @^@@@@          SZ      VU
)@@G@@  A0  @E@@@@          DI,U      A0,6              CONVERT TO WORD COUNT VV
)@@G@@@F@@@@          MSI       A0,*0,X11         TIMES NUMBER OF RECORDS     VW
)@@G@@@E@@@@          JN        A0,ERR1           ERROR IF NEGATIVE     @E@@@@VX
)@@G@@          MI,U      A0,11             ADD 10% SAFETY FACTOR @ @@@@      VY
)@@G@@    DI,U      A0,10     @ @@@@          DSL       A0,36     @D@@@@      VZ
)@@G@@    S         A1,A2             SAVE VALUE.     @E@@@@          DI,U    WA
)@@G@@  A0,114688         GET FILE SIZE IN POS  @F@@@@          JZ        A0,SWB
)@@G@@MALL          JUMP IF LESS THAN 1 POSITION@D@@@@          A,U       A0,1WC
)@@G@@              ROUND UPWARD    @F@@@@          S         A0,XB           WD
)@@G@@  STORE XB SIZE, POSITIONS    @E@@@@          TG,U      A0,XBMAX+1      WE
)@@G@@  MAX XB SIZE EXCEEDED? @E@@@@          J         ERR3              YES,WF
)@@G@@ PRINT ERROR MSG  @F@@@@          L,U       R1,NMGPS          SEARCH MERWG
)@@G@@GE-POWER TABLE    @ @@@@          L         A2,(1,3)  @H@@@@          SGWH
)@@G@@,H2     A0,MGPS-3,*A2     LOOKUP XB SIZE IN MERGE-POWER TABLE     @D@@@@WI
)@@G@@          J         ERR3              MUCH TOO BIG!   @G@@@@          L,WJ
)@@G@@U       A1,0,A2           RESULT, MGP (MERGE-POWER) IN A2   @H@@@@      WK
)@@G@@    MSI,U     A1,1792           FIND AMOUNT OF CORE USING 1792-WD BUFFERWL
)@@G@@@G@@@@          A,U       A1,2791           2791=1792+999 = 1TRK + ROUNDWM
)@@G@@ING   @^@@@@          SZ        A0  @ @@@@          DI,U      A0,1000   WN
)@@G@@@F@@@@          S         A0,CORE           CORE REQUIRED IN THOUSANDS. WO
)@@G@@@H@@@@          MI,U      A0,15000          15 (1.5) IS DEFAULT BIAS, 10WP
)@@G@@00 TO GET WD@H@@@@          AN,U      A1,80640          CALC. EXPECTED SWQ
)@@G@@TRING SIZE,  3*15*1792  @H@@@@          DI,U      A0,19712          11*1WR
)@@G@@792 TO GET TRKS, 11 = 10 ALMOST     @C@@@@          S         A0,A3     WS
)@@G@@        SAVE VALUE@E@@@@          L         A0,XB             NOW CALCULWT
)@@G@@ATE XA SIZE @E@@@@          DSL       A0,30             (CONV POS TO TRKWU
)@@G@@)     @H@@@@          DI,U      A0,0,A2           XA = XB/(MGP)+1 ROUNDEWV
)@@G@@D UP TO STRING SIZ@H@@@@          AU        A0,A3             NOW ROUND WW
)@@G@@UP TO WHOLE EXPECTED ST. SIZE.@^@@@@          SZ        A0  @ @@@@      WX
)@@G@@    DI        A0,A3     @ @@@@          MSI       A0,A3     @E@@@@      WY
)@@G@@    S         A0,XA             STORE XA SIZE, TRKS   @ @@@@          ONWZ
)@@G@@        REMTYPE   @F@@@@          L         A0,XB             LOAD XB SIXA
)@@G@@ZE, IN POSITIONS  @F@@@@          TLE,U     A0,XBMAXF+1       MAX FIXED XB
)@@G@@POS EXCEEDED?     @F@@@@          J         MAVCHK            NO, CHECK XC
)@@G@@MS AVAILABILITY   @F@@@@DISCON    L,U       A0,1              YES, SET RXD
)@@G@@EMOVABLE ASG FLAG @ @@@@          S         A0,DISC   @G@@@@          J XE
)@@G@@        CHEKD             TRY ASSIGNING XB ON REMOBAVLE PACK@ @@@@      XF
)@@G@@    OFF       REMTYPE   @C@@@@MAVCHK    L,U       A0,MSPKT          GET XG
)@@G@@FATBL @ @@@@          ER        MSCON$    @F@@@@          JN        A0,EXH
)@@G@@RR7           IF NO GOOD, HANDLE ERROR    @F@@@@          SZ        A10 XI
)@@G@@              CLEAR TOTAL TRACKS AVAILABLE@G@@@@          SZ        A1  XJ
)@@G@@              CLEAR TOTAL POSITIONS AVAILLABLE  @F@@@@          L       XK
)@@G@@  A2,MSEND          GET LAST MS DEVICE INDEX    @E@@@@          AN      XL
)@@G@@  A2,MSBEG          GET # OF MS TYPES - 1 @D@@@@          TNZ       MSBEXM
)@@G@@G             NEW-TYPE FATBL? @F@@@@          L,U       A2,7            XN
)@@G@@  NO, GET OLD LENGTH OF FATBL @F@@@@FATLOOP   L,H1      A0,MSBUF,A2     XO
)@@G@@  GET INDEX TO STATUS TABLE   @D@@@@          TNZ       MSBEG           XP
)@@G@@  NEW-TYPE FATBL? @F@@@@          JZ        A0,FATEND         NO, IF ZERXQ
)@@G@@O, NONE CONFIGURED@F@@@@          A,H2      A1,MSBUF+2,A0     BUMP AVAILXR
)@@G@@ABLE POSITIONS    @E@@@@          L         A0,MSBUF+1,A0     GET POSITIXS
)@@G@@ONS AVAIL   @F@@@@          LSSL      A0,12             GET RID OF  ROT XT
)@@G@@POINTER     @ @@@@          SSL       A0,12     @E@@@@          A       XU
)@@G@@  A10,A0            BUMP AVAILABLE TRACKS @E@@@@FATEND    JGD       A2,FXV
)@@G@@ATLOOP        HANDLE ALL MS DEVICES @G@@@@          TLE       A1,XB     XW
)@@G@@        ENOUGH POSITIONS FOR THE XB FILE? @E@@@@          DO REMTYPE=0 ,XX
)@@G@@ J ERR6       NO, PRINT ERROR MSG   @F@@@@          DO REMTYPE>0 , J DISXY
)@@G@@CON     NO, SWITCH TO REMOVABLE ASG @F@@@@          L         A1,XB     XZ
)@@G@@        GET POSITIONS NEEDED FOR XB @E@@@@          LSSL      A1,6      YA
)@@G@@        CONVERT TO TRACKS     @F@@@@          A         A1,XA           YB
)@@G@@  ADD TRACKS REQUIRED FOR XA  @B@@@@          A,U       A1,1248         YC
)@@G@@  ??? @F@@@@          TLE       A10,A1            ARE ENOUGH TRACKS AVAIYD
)@@G@@LABLE?@E@@@@          J         ERR5              NO, PRINT ERROR MSG   YE
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @ @@@@.         ASSIGN THE XB FILE  @[@@@@.     @ @@@@CHEKD YF
)@@G@@    L         A0,XB     @F@@@@          JZ        A0,CVXA           SKIPYG
)@@G@@ IF NO XB FILE NEEDED   @F@@@@          LMJ       X11,CV            CONVYH
)@@G@@ERT TO FIELDATA DECIMAL @^@@@@          SZ        A0  @ @@@@          L YI
)@@G@@        A1,A2     @E@@@@          LDSL      A0,0,A3           MOVE INIT YJ
)@@G@@RESV TO A0  @A@@@@          L         A1,('/POS/ ')   @G@@@@          DSYK
)@@G@@L       A0,6              MOVE LAST CHAR OF INIT RESV TO A1 @G@@@@      YL
)@@G@@    AN,U      A3,6              DECREMENT SHIFT COUNT BY 1 CHAR   @F@@@@YM
)@@G@@          DSL       A1,0,A3           SHIFT X/POS/ AND MAX GRAN   @H@@@@YN
)@@G@@          SSC       A0,0,A3           ADJUST REMAINING CHARS OF INIT RESYO
)@@G@@V     @G@@@@          A         A1,A0             ADD REMAINING INIT RESYP
)@@G@@V CHARS     @G@@@@          DS        A1,ASGXB+3        STORE XXX/POS/XXYQ
)@@G@@X IN ASG IMAGE    @F@@@@          LA        A0,(FTYPE)        GET FIXED YR
)@@G@@XB EQUIP TYPE     @E@@@@          SA        A0,ASGXB+2        STORE IN AYS
)@@G@@SG IMAGE    @E@@@@          L         A1,(ASGXBL,ASGXB) GET IMAGE LENGTHYT
)@@G@@, ADDR@ @@@@          ON        REMTYPE   @F@@@@          TNZ       DISCYU
)@@G@@              AH!  SHOULD WE DO REM ASG?  @E@@@@          J         DOITYV
)@@G@@              NO, ASSIGN AS FIXED   @F@@@@          L         A2,(RTYPE)YW
)@@G@@        GET DESIRED REM EQUIP TYPE  @E@@@@          S         A2,ASGXB+2YX
)@@G@@        STORE IN ASG IMAGE    @[@@@@.     @B@@@@.         ADD A COMMA FOYY
)@@G@@R PACKID CLAUSE   @[@@@@.     @F@@@@          SZ        A2              YZ
)@@G@@  A3=INIT RESV BIT COUNT - 6  @E@@@@          DI,U      A2,6            ZA
)@@G@@  CONVERT TO CHAR COUNT @D@@@@          L,U       A0,','            GET ZB
)@@G@@A COMMA     @F@@@@          EX        COMMA,A2          STORE COMMA IN AZC

)@@G@@RAM   @[@@@@.     @D@@@@.         SUBROUTINE TO DISPLAY AND ISSUE CSF$ RAQ
)@@G@@EQUEST@[@@@@.     @H@@@@.         ENTER WITH A1 = IMAGE LENGTH,ADDRESS  AR

)@@G@@SORT) @^@@@@          J         SM2 @E@@@@SM0       MI,U      A1,1792   CI

)@@G@@RT WITH 2K OF CORE)     @H@@@@          L         A2,A1             NOW CL

)@@G@@ SDF OUTPUT ROUTINE     @[@@@@.     @F@@@@. CALLED IF W-OPTION IS SET.  MG
)@@G@@WRITES EACH QUALIFIER*FILENAME(CYC) @F@@@@. INTO SDF FILE WHOSE NAME IS MH
)@@G@@DEFINED BY CONFIG PARAMETER 'WFILE'.@[@@@@.     @^@@@@          AXR$    MI

)@@G@@        1,0 @ @@@@          +         05001,0,0 @[@@@@/$(1).@[@@@@.     MU
)@@G@@@C@@@@. SDF INITIALIZATION:  SET UP FCT AND OPEN SDFO @[@@@@.     @E@@@@MV

)@@G@@OUT IF NO GOOD    @ @@@@          LA,U      A0,06     @E@@@@          SANB
)@@G@@,T1     A0,FCT+10         SET TO WRITE 6 WORDS  @F@@@@          LA,U    NC

)@@G@@*[S@@@*SDFF*@F@@@@. @MFD SNAP$ ROUTINE - DUMPS DIRECTORY ITEMS SELECTED QC
)@@G@@BY THE USER @[@@@@.     @^@@@@          AXR$      .   @G@@@@          COQD
)@@G@@NFIG    .                 DEFINE CONFIGURATION PARAMTERES   @ @@@@      QE
)@@G@@    ON        SNAPOK    @D@@@@          EQUFS     .                 DEFIQF
)@@G@@NE TAGS     @D@@@@PRT       FORM      12,6,18           FORM T1,S3,H2   QG
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @^@@@@P         PROC      1   @^@@@@SNAPP*    NAME      0   QH
)@@G@@@^@@@@SETSNAP*  NAME      1   @F@@@@          DO P(1)=0 , GO ERONLY     QI
)@@G@@  SKIP IF NO PARAMETERS GIVEN @D@@@@          LA        A0,(P(1,1))     QJ
)@@G@@  GET HEADER INFO @H@@@@          DO OLDMFD=0 , GO ON         SKIP 'DAD'QK
)@@G@@ CHECK IF NEW FORMAT ONLY     @E@@@@       DO 1-(P(1,1)='DAD   ') , GO OQL
)@@G@@N SKIP IF NOT 'DAD'     @E@@@@          TNZ       MFD$F             NEW QM
)@@G@@FORMAT DIRECTORY? @G@@@@          LA        A0,('GTB   ')     NO, USE 'GQN
)@@G@@TB' RATHER THAN 'DAD'   @^@@@@ON        NAME      .   @E@@@@          SAQO
)@@G@@        A0,SNAPKT         STORE IN SNAP$ PACKET @E@@@@          LA,U    QP
)@@G@@  A0,P(1,2)         GET BUFFER ADDRESS    @F@@@@          SA        A0,BQQ
)@@G@@UFAD          STORE IT IN SNAP$ PACKET    @H@@@@          DO P(1)<3 , GOQR
)@@G@@ ERONLY       IF NOT SPECIFIED, LEAVE # WORDS AS IS   @F@@@@          LAQS
)@@G@@,U      A0,P(1,3)         BUT IF SPECIFIED, USE IT    @E@@@@          SAQT
)@@G@@        A0,NWRDS          SET # OF WORDS TO SNAP@^@@@@ERONLY    NAME    QU
)@@G@@  .   @G@@@@          DO P(0,0)>0 , GO AWAY       SKIP IF JUST SETTING UQV
)@@G@@P PACKET    @ @@@@          ON        SNAPSUB=0 @F@@@@          LA,U    QW
)@@G@@  A0,SNAPKT         GET SNAP$ PACKET ADDRESS    @D@@@@          ER      QX
)@@G@@  SNAP$             DO THE SNAP$    @ @@@@          OFF       SNAPSUB=0 QY
)@@G@@@ @@@@          ON        SNAPSUB   @D@@@@          LMJ       X10,SNAP$ QZ
)@@G@@        DO THE SNAP$    @D@@@@          LA        A2,SNAP           RELORA
)@@G@@AD SNAP BITS@ @@@@          OFF       SNAPSUB   @G@@@@          SR      RB
)@@G@@  R15,SNAPKT+2      SET SNAPPED-SOMETHING INDICATOR   @C@@@@          DORC
)@@G@@ (P(1,1)='LI0')++(P(1,1)='LI1') , ; @F@@@@          SR        R15,LISNPDRD
)@@G@@        SET LEAD-ITEM-SNAPPED FLAG  @^@@@@AWAY      NAME      .   @#@@@@RE
)@@G@@          END     @[@@@@.     @D@@@@SNAPKT    'SEC   '                  RF
)@@G@@  SNAP$ PACKET    @D@@@@          +         28,0              ASSUME 1 SRG
)@@G@@ECTOR @^@@@@          +         0   @E@@@@NWRDS     EQUF      SNAPKT+1,,RH
)@@G@@H1      # OF WORDS TO SNAP    @F@@@@BUFAD     EQUF      SNAPKT+1,,H2    RI
)@@G@@  ADDRESS OF BUFFER TO SNAP   @[@@@@.     @ @@@@          ON        CHKPRJ
)@@G@@CT=0  @C@@@@TEMPGT    'TEMP FILE DAD SNAP NOT CONFIGURED'   @B@@@@TEMPGTRK
)@@G@@P   +         0200+($-TEMPGT),TEMPGT@ @@@@          OFF       CHKPCT=0  RL
)@@G@@@ @@@@          ON        CHKPCT    @E@@@@TDAD      ' SNAP OF DAD ITEMS RM

)@@G@@ROUTINE     @ @@@@/         ON        POLDBG    @[@@@@.     @#@@@@. DEBUWR
)@@G@@G SNAPS     @[@@@@.     @G@@@@POLDBM    'TESTS = &   AOX = &   POLNTH = WS
)@@G@@&   SORT = &   BRKCNT = &'    @F@@@@SSIZE     EQU       6               WT
)@@G@@  SUPER SPEC TABLE ENTRY SIZE @E@@@@BRKSIZ    EQU       6               WU
)@@G@@  BRKTBL ENTRY SIZE     @[@@@@.     @]@@@@SN900*    . @C@@@@          E$WV

)@@G@@0)      SKIP A LINE     @G@@@@          L$OAD     INSEG,IN2020,1    RETUXI
)@@G@@RN TO INITIALIZATION SEGMENT  @ @@@@          OFF       POLDBG    @ @@@@XJ
)@@G@@/         ON        SNAPSUB   @[@@@@.     @F@@@@. THIS SUBROUTINE PEFORMXK
)@@G@@S A MORE READABLE SNAP$-TYPE DUMP THAN IS @G@@@@. AVAILABLE THROUGH ER SXL
)@@G@@NAP$.  IT INCLUDES A SHORTER FORMAT FOR DEMAND  @H@@@@. USE.  THIS ROUTIXM
)@@G@@NE IS USED ONLY IF CONFIG PARAMETER 'SNAPSUB' IS NONZERO.   @[@@@@.     XN
)@@G@@@A@@@@.    ENTER VIA:  LMJ  X10,SNAP$     @G@@@@.     DESTROYS:  X4, X10XO
)@@G@@, X11, A6, R2, R4, PLUS REGISTERS USED BY EDIT$ @[@@@@.     @]@@@@$(0)  XP
)@@G@@    . @ @@@@ENTIRE    'ALL & WORDS = &'   @G@@@@LASTWD    RES       1   XQ
)@@G@@              LAST WORD OF EACH LINE IS STORED  @E@@@@.                 XR
)@@G@@                    HERE FOR COMPARISON   @E@@@@WPL       RES       1   XS
)@@G@@              # OF WORDS PER LINE   @[@@@@.     @F@@@@SLEN      EQU     XT
)@@G@@  5                 WORDS/LINE FOR SHORT LISTING@F@@@@LLEN      EQU     XU
)@@G@@  8                 WORDS/LINE FOR LONG LISTING @[@@@@.     @]@@@@$(1),SXV
)@@G@@NAP$. @E@@@@          P$RINT    ( PRT 2,1,SNAPKT) PRINT SNAP HEADER     XW
)@@G@@@F@@@@          LA        A0,NWRDS          GET NUMBER OF WORDS TO SNAP XX
)@@G@@@F@@@@          AND,U     A0,077777         MASK OF XAR BITS TO BE SAFE XY
)@@G@@@F@@@@          JZ        A1,,X10           IF NO WORDS TO SNAP, RETURN XZ
)@@G@@@G@@@@          SA        A1,NWRDS          OTHERWISE, PUT MASKED # WORDYA
)@@G@@S BACK@E@@@@          LX        X4,(1,0)          INITIALIZE WORD INDEX YB
)@@G@@@E@@@@          AX        X4,BUFAD          ADD BUFFER ADDRESS    @G@@@@YC
)@@G@@          TLE,U     A1,4              IF ONLY 1-3 WORDS BEING SNAPPED,  YD
)@@G@@@F@@@@          J         NOTSAM               SKIP ALL-THE-SAME TEST   YE
)@@G@@@F@@@@          AN,U      A1,1              MINUS 1 FOR SEARCH COUNT    YF
)@@G@@@D@@@@          SA        A1,R1             SET SEARCH COUNT@H@@@@      YG
)@@G@@    LX        A2,X4             COPY WORD INDEX AND INCREMENT TO A2     YH
)@@G@@@E@@@@          LA        A0,0,A2           GET 1ST WORD OF AREA  @F@@@@YI
)@@G@@          SNE       A0,1,*A2          FIND ANY DIFFERENT WORDS?   @D@@@@YJ
)@@G@@          J         $+2               NO, ALL THE SAME@E@@@@          J YK
)@@G@@        NOTSAM            YES, NOT ALL THE SAME @[@@@@.     @D@@@@. THE YL
)@@G@@ENTIRE AREA IS EQUAL:  PRINT MESSAGE AND RETURN @[@@@@.     @C@@@@      YM
)@@G@@    E$DIT     EDPACK            OPEN EDIT @C@@@@          E$MSG     ENTIYN
)@@G@@RE            START MSG @E@@@@          E$DECV    NWRDS             EDITYO
)@@G@@ NUMBER OF WORDS  @D@@@@          E$MSGR    .                 CONTINUE MYP
)@@G@@SG    @C@@@@          E$OCTV    0,X4              ADD VALUE @C@@@@      YQ
)@@G@@    P$RINT    POUT              PRINT MSG @C@@@@          J         0,X1YR
)@@G@@0             RETURN    @[@@@@.     @D@@@@. ENTIRE AREA IS NOT EQUAL:  DYS
)@@G@@UMP IT LINE BY LINE     @[@@@@.     @E@@@@NOTSAM    LA        A0,( PRT 1YT
)@@G@@,0,0)   GET SET TO SKIP A LINE@D@@@@          TZ        LONGLIST        YU
)@@G@@  LONG LISTING?   @C@@@@          ER        PRINT$            YES, DO ITYV
)@@G@@@E@@@@          LA        A0,NWRDS          GET # OF WORDS TO SNAP@E@@@@YW
)@@G@@          DSL       A0,36             GET SET FOR DIVIDE    @E@@@@      YX
)@@G@@    LA,U      A2,SLEN           GET SHORT WORDS/LINE  @D@@@@          TZYY
)@@G@@        LONGLIST          LONG LISTING?   @F@@@@          LA,U      A2,LYZ
)@@G@@LEN           YES, GET LONG WORDS/LINE    @E@@@@          SA        A2,WZA
)@@G@@PL            STORE WORDS PER LINE  @F@@@@          DI        A0,A2     ZB
)@@G@@        CALCULATE # OF LINES NEEDED @F@@@@          TZ        A1        ZC
)@@G@@        REMAINDER ON PARTIAL LINE?  @B@@@@          AA,U      A0,1      ZD
)@@G@@        YES @D@@@@          ANA,U     A0,1              ADJUST FOR JGD  ZE
)@@G@@@D@@@@          SA        A0,R4             SET LOOP COUNT  @F@@@@      ZF
)@@G@@    LA,U      A6,0              INITIALIZE SKIP INDICATOR   @F@@@@      ZG
)@@G@@    J         PRINTLINE         ALWAYS PRINT FIRST LINE     @[@@@@.     ZH
)@@G@@@H@@@@. BEFORE PRINTING EACH LINE (EXCEPT THE FIRST AND LAST LINES), CHEZI
)@@G@@CK TO SEE   @H@@@@. IF ALL WORDS ON THIS LINE ARE EQUAL TO THE LAST WORDZJ
)@@G@@ OF THE PREVIOUS LINE.  @H@@@@. IF SO, DO NOT PRINT THIS LINE, BUT INDICZK
)@@G@@ATE, VIA A '*' ON THE NEXT PRINTED  @C@@@@. LINE, THAT AT LEAST ONE LINEZL
)@@G@@ HAS BEEN SKIPPED.@[@@@@.     @D@@@@LINELOOP  LA        A0,R4           ZM
)@@G@@  GET LINE NUMBER @F@@@@          JZ        A0,PRINTLINE      IF LAST LIZN
)@@G@@NE, DON'T SKIP IT @F@@@@          LR        R1,WPL            GET # OF WZO
)@@G@@ORDS PER LINE     @G@@@@          LA        A0,LASTWD         GET LAST WZP
)@@G@@ORD FROM PREVIOUS LINE  @H@@@@          LX        A1,X4             COPYZQ
)@@G@@ CURRENT INDEX AND INCREMENT TO A1  @G@@@@          SNE       A0,0,*A1  ZR
)@@G@@        ANYTHING DIFFERENT ON THIS LINE?  @E@@@@          J         $+2 ZS
)@@G@@              NO, SKIP THIS LINE    @E@@@@          J         PRINTLINE ZT
)@@G@@        YES, PRINT THIS LINE  @E@@@@          LA,U      A6,1            ZU
)@@G@@  SET SKIP INDICATOR    @E@@@@          AX        X4,WPL            POINZV
)@@G@@T TO NEXT LINE    @D@@@@          J         NEXTLINE          SKIP THIS ZW
)@@G@@LINE  @[@@@@.     @E@@@@. WE DON'T WANT TO SKIP THIS LINE:  COMPOSE AND ZX
)@@G@@PRINT IT    @[@@@@.     @C@@@@PRINTLINE E$DIT     EDPACK            OPENZY
)@@G@@ EDIT @F@@@@          LR        R2,A6             HOLD PREVIOUS SKIP INDZZ
)@@G@@ICATOR@F@@@@          LA,U      A6,0              CLEAR NEW SKIP INDICATAA
)@@G@@OR    @G@@@@          LA,U      A0,0,X4           GET INDEX OF FIRST WORAB
)@@G@@D IN LINE   @E@@@@          ANA       A0,BUFAD          MAKE IT RELATIVEAC
)@@G@@ TO 0 @D@@@@          E$OCTF    4                 EDIT THE NUMBER @D@@@@AD
)@@G@@          E$SKIP    1                 SKIP A SPACE    @E@@@@          LAAE
)@@G@@,U      A0,' '            ASSUME ANOTHER SPACE  @G@@@@          TZ      AF
)@@G@@  R2                BUT WAS SKIP FLAG PREVIOUSLY SET? @F@@@@          LAAG
)@@G@@,U      A0,'*'            YES, INDICATE SKIPPED LINES @F@@@@          E$AH
)@@G@@CHAR    .                 EDIT A SPACE OR ASTERISK    @F@@@@          LRAI
)@@G@@        R2,WPL            GET # OF WORDS PER LINE     @D@@@@          JGAJ
)@@G@@D       R2,$+1            LESS 1 FOR JGD  @[@@@@.     @H@@@@. EDIT PROPEAK
)@@G@@R NUMBER OF WORDS PER LINE.  THE LAST LINE MAY BE A PARTIAL LINE. @[@@@@AL
)@@G@@.     @G@@@@WORDLOOP  E$OCTF    12,0,*X4          EDIT VALUE AND POINT TAM
)@@G@@O NEXT WORD @E@@@@          E$SKIP    2                 2 SPACES BETWEENAN
)@@G@@ WORDS@E@@@@          LA,U      A0,0,X4           GET CURRENT WORD INDEXAO
)@@G@@@E@@@@          ANA       A0,BUFAD          MAKE IT RELATIVE TO 0 @D@@@@AP
)@@G@@          TLE       A0,NWRDS          ALL DONE YET?   @F@@@@.           AQ
)@@G@@                          IF SO, MAY BE PARTIAL LINE  @G@@@@          JGAR
)@@G@@D       R2,WORDLOOP       NO, GO BACK AND FINISH THIS LINE  @G@@@@      AS
)@@G@@    P$RINT    POUT              DONE WITH THIS LINE:  PRINT IT    @[@@@@AT
)@@G@@.     @H@@@@. SAVE LAST WORD OF THIS LINE FOR SKIP COMPARISON, AND SET FAU
)@@G@@OR NEXT LINE.     @[@@@@.     @E@@@@NEXTLINE  LA,U      A0,0,X4         AV
)@@G@@  GET CURRENT WORD INDEX@F@@@@          ANA,U     A0,1              BACKAW
)@@G@@ UP TO LAST WORD PRINTED@G@@@@          LA        A0,0,A0           PICKAX
)@@G@@ UP THE LAST WORD PRINTED     @F@@@@          SA        A0,LASTWD       AY
)@@G@@  AND STORE IT FOR SKIP TEST  @E@@@@          JGD       R4,LINELOOP     AZ
)@@G@@  MORE LINES?  DO THEM  @F@@@@          J         0,X10             ALL BA
)@@G@@DONE:  RETURN TO CALLER @ @@@@          OFF       SNAPSUB   @ @@@@      BB
)@@G@@    OFF       SNAPOK    @#@@@@          END     ___T TO A1  @G@@@@      BC
)@@G@@*[S@@@*SDFF*@A@@@@. @MFD INITIALIZATION - PHASE 1     @[@@@@.     @G@@@@BD
)@@G@@. ALL USE OF INFOR$ MUST BE COMPLETE BY THE END OF THIS ROUTINE, SINCE  BE
)@@G@@@G@@@@. INFOR$ IS COLLECTED IN THE INIT1 SEGMENT, WHICH GETS OVERLAID AFBF

)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @F@@@@. MOST OF THE SPECS WITH ASSUMED VALUES HAVE SINGLE-BISE
)@@G@@T VALUES AND@D@@@@. TESTS.  FOR THESE, WE WILL DO A SINGLE-BIT SORT.    SF

)@@G@@.                                     IS 2**5 (040), A2=0 BECAUSE @G@@@@SQ
)@@G@@.                                     THE MS BIT IS ALREADY CORRECT     SR

)@@G@@              LEFT-JUSTIFY IN H2    @G@@@@          AA,U      A2,X8     TW

)@@G@@     OR TEP?@B@@@@          J         $+2               YES @D@@@@      UQ

)@@G@@  A3,( LMJ X11,BRKBIT)  GET AN 'LMJ X11,BRKBIT' INSTR @D@@@@IN1280    LAUS
)@@G@@        A0,BRKPNT         GET TABLE INDEX @E@@@@          NOP       0,0,UT
)@@G@@*A0           ADJUST FOR NEW ENTRY  @G@@@@          DS        A2,BRKLOADUU
)@@G@@,A0     STORE LOAD AND TEST INSTRUCTIONS  @G@@@@          SA        A1,BUV

)@@G@@        A1,TB4SPEC,X9     GET 1ST 3 CHARS OF SPEC (FOR H2)  @F@@@@      UY

)@@G@@NT          . INCREMENT BREAK COUNT BY 1  @ @@@@          OFF       BRKOVF
)@@G@@K     @F@@@@IN1290    TZ        TB4VAL            SPEC WITH ASSUMED VALUVG
)@@G@@E?    @F@@@@          J         IN1080            YES, USER WANTS SORT OVH
)@@G@@N IT, @F@@@@.                                     SO THAT'S ALL WE DO WIVI
)@@G@@TH IT @]@@@@IN1300    . @ @@@@          OFF       SORTOK    @F@@@@      VJ
)@@G@@    TNZ       TB4VAL            ASSUMED VALUE FOR THIS ITEM?@C@@@@      VK
)@@G@@    J         IN1310            NO, GO ON @[@@@@.     @F@@@@. DON'T PERMVL
)@@G@@IT USER TO OVERRIDE OPERATION, J-DESIGNATOR, ETC., FOR@B@@@@. THE SPECIAVM

)@@G@@  NO, HANDLE POSSIBLE ERROR   @[@@@@.     @F@@@@. NOTE THAT THE ABOVE TEVY
)@@G@@ST WILL NOT WORK PROPERLY IF THE ASSUMED  @B@@@@. TEST FOR AN ITEM IS TZVZ
)@@G@@, TNZ, TP, OR TN. @[@@@@.     @E@@@@          LA        A2,TB4OP        WA

)@@G@@  X10,SPECER        NO OPERATION, AND NOT SNAP OR SORT@[@@@@.     @D@@@@WL
)@@G@@. DETERMINE WHICH WORD OF DIRECTORY ITEM TO CHECK     @[@@@@.     @D@@@@WM

)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @E@@@@. SUBROUTINE TO RETURN SORT RECORD WORD # IN A2, BASEDXA
)@@G@@ ON   @A@@@@. SPECIFIED+ASSUMED ITEM OFFSET.    @[@@@@.     @A@@@@.     XB
)@@G@@  ENTER VIA:  LMJ  X10,IN1340 @ @@@@.                   <RETURN>  @[@@@@XC
)@@G@@.     @A@@@@.        DESTROYS:  A0, A2, X10     @[@@@@.     @E@@@@IN1340XD
)@@G@@    LA,U      A2,0              INITIALIZE WORD #     @E@@@@          LAXE
)@@G@@,S3     A0,ELT$           FCYCLE CHAR COUNT     @E@@@@          JZ      XF

)@@G@@D OFFSET    @D@@@@          LA        A0,TB4ITM         GET ITEM INDEX  XQ

)@@G@@RD    @ @@@@          AA        A2,A0     @E@@@@          J         0,X1XS
)@@G@@0             RETURN WORD # IN A2   @[@@@@.     @F@@@@IN1400    SA,H2   XT
)@@G@@  A2,SSLOAD,X6      STORE IN SUPER SPEC TABLE   @[@@@@.     @ @@@@. CHECXU
)@@G@@K FOR LEGAL OPERATION   @[@@@@.     @E@@@@          LA,H1     A0,ELT$+7 XV
)@@G@@        GET OPERATION (RKEY)  @D@@@@          LR,U      R1,OPCODL       XW
)@@G@@  # OF OPCODES    @E@@@@          LA        A3,(1,0)          FROM OPCODXX
)@@G@@E TABLE     @C@@@@          SE,H1     A0,OPCODE,*A3     FIND?     @C@@@@XY
)@@G@@          LMJ       X10,SPECER        NO, ERROR @G@@@@          LA,U    XZ

)@@G@@OR GIVEN?   @F@@@@          LMJ       X10,SPECER        YES, CAN'T HAVE YD
)@@G@@J-DES ON DTE@E@@@@          TNZ,S1    ELT$+1            WAS A VALUE GIVEYE
)@@G@@N?    @E@@@@          LMJ       X10,SPECER        NO, MUST HAVE A VALUE YF
)@@G@@@F@@@@          LA        A0,INITDTE        GET INITIAL DTE INSTRUCTION YG
)@@G@@@G@@@@          AA        A0,X6             POINT TO PROPER SSPVAL TABLEYH
)@@G@@ ADDR @F@@@@          SA        A0,SSTEST,X6      STORE IN SUPER SPEC TAYI
)@@G@@BLE   @F@@@@          LA,H1     A0,( DL A0,0,X8)  GET A 'DL A0,X,X8' INSYJ
)@@G@@TR    @E@@@@          SA,H1     A0,SSLOAD,X6      CHANGE 'LA' TO 'DL'   YK
)@@G@@@C@@@@          J         IN1490            CONTINUE  @[@@@@.     @^@@@@YL
)@@G@@. OPERATION IS NOT DTE  @[@@@@.     @F@@@@IN1440    LA,S4     A0,OPCODE-YM
)@@G@@1,A3    GET OCTAL CODE FOR THIS OP  @G@@@@          SA,S1     A0,SSTEST,YN
)@@G@@X6      STORE IT IN REMOTE TEST INSTR     @[@@@@.     @B@@@@. CHECK FOR YO
)@@G@@LEGAL J-DESIGNATOR, IF GIVEN  @[@@@@.     @F@@@@          TZ,S5     ELT$YP

)@@G@@PER SPEC TABLE    @D@@@@          SSL       A0,8              MOVE J BACZF
)@@G@@K     @[@@@@.     @ @@@@. OPCODE INDEX REMAINS IN A10 @[@@@@.     @G@@@@ZG
)@@G@@. ASSUME SPECIFIED TEST VALUE IS FIELDATA, AND STORE IT.  IF NECESSARY, ZH
)@@G@@@F@@@@. SET SHIFT VALUE (SSHIFT) TO PERMIT SPECS LIKE  MI0(7)/TE/S1.C  .ZI
)@@G@@@[@@@@.     @G@@@@IN1490    DL        A2,ELT$+9         GET SUPER SPEC EZJ

)@@G@@ SHIFT COUNT@G@@@@.                                     VALUE IS ALREADYZS

)@@G@@. CHECK FOR MASK BEING SPECIFIED.  IF SO, SET MASK IN SUPER SPEC TABLE  AG

)@@G@@ITH THIS SPEC     @[@@@@.     @ @@@@. DATE CONVERSION SUBROUTINE  @[@@@@CP

)@@G@@R Y   @C@@@@          LMJ       X10,SPECER        NO GOOD   @D@@@@      DE
)@@G@@    LX,U      X2,ELT$+9         ADDR OF SPEC    @[@@@@.     @ @@@@. TRY DF
)@@G@@M/D/Y IN 1ST CHAR FIRST @[@@@@.     @E@@@@          LA,S1     A2,ELT$+9 DG
)@@G@@        GET FIRST CHAR OF ELT @H@@@@          LX        X1,(1,1)        DH
)@@G@@  SET FOR NUMBER STARTING WITH 2ND CHAR   @[@@@@.     @#@@@@. CHECK FOR DI
)@@G@@M/D/Y @[@@@@.     @C@@@@IN1707A   TE,U      A2,'M'            MONTH?    DJ
)@@G@@@B@@@@          TNE,U     A2,'D'            DAY?@D@@@@          J       DK
)@@G@@  IN1707B           ONE OF THE ABOVE@C@@@@          TNE,U     A2,'Y'    DL
)@@G@@        OR YEAR?  @B@@@@          J         IN1707B           YES @[@@@@DM
)@@G@@.     @G@@@@. CHAR IS NOT M/D/Y.  IF FIRST TIME THRU, TRY LAST CHAR.  ELDN
)@@G@@SE, ERROR   @[@@@@.     @D@@@@          TNZ,U     0,X1              FIRSDO
)@@G@@T TIME THRU?@C@@@@          LMJ       X10,SPECER        NO, ERROR @F@@@@DP
)@@G@@          EX        ACLD-1,A3         PICK UP LAST CHAR OF SPEC   @D@@@@DQ
)@@G@@          SA        A0,A2             STORE IN A2     @G@@@@          JGDR
)@@G@@D       X1,IN1707A        TRY ALT FORMAT (M/D/Y AFTER #)    @[@@@@.     DS
)@@G@@@D@@@@. FOUND M/D/Y.  NOW CHECK FOR 1-4 DIGIT DECIMAL NUMBER@[@@@@.     DT
)@@G@@@D@@@@IN1707B   SSL       A2,3              D=1, M=2, Y=3   @F@@@@      DU
)@@G@@    AN,U      A3,2              ONE LESS CHAR, -1 FOR JGD   @D@@@@      DV
)@@G@@    LA,U      A1,0              INITIALIZE TOTAL@F@@@@          LMJ     DW
)@@G@@  X11,IN1752        CONVERT DEC NUMBER TO BINARY@D@@@@          LMJ     DX
)@@G@@  X10,SPECER        NOT DEC NUMBER  @[@@@@.     @D@@@@. SPEC IS CONVERTEDY
)@@G@@D TO BINARY - RESULT IS IN SSPVAL,X6@[@@@@.     @D@@@@          ER      DZ
)@@G@@  TDATE$            GET TODAY'S DATE@E@@@@          DSL       A0,24     EA
)@@G@@        GET MON,DAY IN A0     @D@@@@          SA,T3     A0,TODAY        EB
)@@G@@  STORE MON,DAY   @C@@@@          SSL       A1,30             GET YEAR  EC
)@@G@@@F@@@@          SA,S4     A1,TODAY          STORE YR IN YR,MON,DAY FMT  ED
)@@G@@@G@@@@          EX        DATJ-1,A2         JUMP TO PROPER ROUTINE FOR MEE
)@@G@@/D/Y  @[@@@@.     @[@@@@. DAY @[@@@@.     @D@@@@          LA        A0,SEF
)@@G@@SPVAL,X6      GET DAYS SPEC'D @E@@@@          DSL       A0,36           EG
)@@G@@  PREPARE FOR DIVIDE    @F@@@@          DI,U      A0,30             DIVIEH
)@@G@@DE BY # OF DAYS IN MONTH@D@@@@          LA,S6     A2,TODAY          CURREI
)@@G@@ENT DAY     @E@@@@          AN        A2,A1             SUBTRACT # OF DAEJ
)@@G@@YS    @D@@@@          TG,U      A2,1              NEG OR ZERO?    @B@@@@EK
)@@G@@          J         $+3               NO  @F@@@@          A,U       A2,3EL
)@@G@@0             YES, SET FOR PREVIOUS MONTH @E@@@@          A,U       A0,1EM
)@@G@@              ADD 1 TO MONTH COUNT  @E@@@@          SA        A0,SSPVAL,EN
)@@G@@X6      STORE MONTH COUNT     @D@@@@          SA,S6     A2,TODAY        EO
)@@G@@  STORE NEW DAY   @[@@@@.     @]@@@@. MONTH     @[@@@@.     @D@@@@IN1708EP
)@@G@@    LA        A0,SSPVAL,X6      MONTH COUNT     @D@@@@          DSL     EQ
)@@G@@  A0,36             SET FOR DIVIDE  @G@@@@          DI,U      A0,12     ER
)@@G@@        DIVIDE BY # OF MONTHS IN YEAR     @D@@@@          LA,S5     A2,TES
)@@G@@ODAY          CURRENT MONTH   @E@@@@          AN        A2,A1           ET
)@@G@@  SUBTRACT # OF MONTHS  @D@@@@          TG,U      A2,1              NEG EU
)@@G@@OR ZERO?    @B@@@@      *[S@@[*SDFF*:[@@@@@@@@@E@A@@@@C@)^@,^@)^@)^[#CLMEV
